#<Spintastic>

    #<Description>

        By Aaron0000

        Vladof barrels just seem to make everything better (unless you're the Buffalo), so I made a lot of guns have Vladof barrels.

        Enable the guns of your choice, as they're all off by default.

    #</Description>

    #<Anarchtastic>
